  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer12157277819734263048">WARNING: Do not read this book unless you have your significant other available or a vibrator with A LOT of batteries!!<br/><br/>**SPOILERS**<br/><br/>Oh my fu*k*ng gosh!   <span id="freeText12157277819734263048" style="display:none">WARNING: Do not read this book unless you have your significant other available or a vibrator with A LOT of batteries!!<br /><br />**SPOILERS**<br /><br />Oh my fu*k*ng gosh! How much sex can you get in one book??? Apparently a bloody lot!<br /><br />I had been reading some really sweet romance novels lately and thought I would give my inner skank a break from the gushiness to have some sexy fun. That sure did happen – however, there was so much sex even my inner skank blushed.<br /><br />As a whole I enjoyed the book, it was sexy as hell, God damn HOT sex scenes, but just too damn many of them. <br /><br />The story sorta felt like :wake up, sex, breakfast, sex, lunch, sex, go for a walk, sex, dinner, sex.<br /><br />But yet the sex always seemed to be new. There was vaginal, anal, oral, sex with toys, sex with food, sex in public places, sex with people watching, a threesome and much, much, more.<br /><br />I think if you take out all the sex scenes there would probably only be about 50 pages of actual storyline and the storyline in itself was quite predictable.<br /><br />All in all it was a HOT HOT HOT read, Olivia Cunning is one talented sex writer but this book is definitely not for the faint of heart.<br /><br />There is an additional video that I found that goes with this my review. Check out my full review at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://riverinaromantics.blogspot.com/2011/05/backstage-pass-by-olivia-cunning.html">http://riverinaromantics.blogspot.com...</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="12157277819734263048" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer177152962" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15224586200613160003">Well. This book had its moments but it left a bad taste in my mouth. <br/><br/>Let’s see. The things that didn’t sit well with me:<br/><br/>Myrna. What a bitch. She’s been through a lot, I give her that, but then again that’s what shrinks are for. She keeps projecting her negative experiences to her “relationship” or however she wants to call it, with Brian. The <i>“you’re a whore, Myrna”</i> chant really got on my nerves from a certain point onwards. Myrna may be a human sexuality professor but she’s full of unresolved c</span>
  <span id="freeText15224586200613160003" style="display:none">Well. This book had its moments but it left a bad taste in my mouth. <br /><br />Let’s see. The things that didn’t sit well with me:<br /><br />Myrna. What a bitch. She’s been through a lot, I give her that, but then again that’s what shrinks are for. She keeps projecting her negative experiences to her “relationship” or however she wants to call it, with Brian. The <i>“you’re a whore, Myrna”</i> chant really got on my nerves from a certain point onwards. Myrna may be a human sexuality professor but she’s full of unresolved complexes and inhibitions. We got it. <br /><br />And this takes me to the next thing I didn’t like: I wasn’t convinced by the way the two main characters hooked up. OK, he may be a famous rock star but he is piss drunk, ridiculing himself in the middle of a hotel bar. She’s a respected college professor who has just wrapped up a conference presentation. And what does she do? She invites him to her room mere minutes after he spends a considerable amount of time worshipping the porcelain god in the hotel’s public restrooms.<br /><br />Another major issue was Brian considering Myrna special. I didn't see how she could be so special after all. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She was good in bed and he heard music when he did her, but other than that her general behaviour was that of any love-struck groupie: she had sex with him before you could say Jack Robinson; she agreed to walk around the hotel and to the band’s suite in nothing but a bathrobe and pink lacy knickers, and then stand practically naked in front of the other band members; she had sex with him (again) in a bath tub while another band member watched and wanked off coming in her hair; she had anal sex with him (yet again) on the suite’s dining table while another band member provided lube. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />As regards sex. I get it. The author wanted to squeeze in as much of it as possible. This is erotica after all. But making your heroes horny all the time and have sex for hours and hours every day doesn’t leave you much space to develop them properly. That’s probably why Brian is a 28-year-old teenager (he falls in love with every single girl he has sex with) with trust issues because the girls he thinks he loves go on to sleep with the band’s hot frontman, Sed. Well, duh. That’s what happens when you fall for featherbrained groupies. And like a typical lovesick juvenile, he puts up with Myrna’s bitchy behaviour time and time again when he should have shown her the door after the first couple of days.<br /><br />The sex itself was ok, though I didn’t see the need for that mediocre BDSM scene. It was lukewarm and clumsy and I could have done without it.<br /><br />The whole <i>“Brian’s parents are shallow has-beens who don’t support him enough emotionally”</i> situation. I have no words. A mild bitchslap from Myrna, the new girlfriend who they'd just met, led to more results than years of Brian’s efforts. Wow. She should change her name to Wonderwoman.<br /><br />The threesome. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was enjoying the scene and was finding the DP while the two men kiss passionately a damn fine mental image when that unbelievable turn-off of a person, Myrna, went all “Brian’s mine and I’m not sharing him” and ruined everything. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I thought that at last, both Brian and Myrna could overcome their trust issues a little. They were having a threesome for hell’s sake. But no. None of that. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Plus, the author introduces the possible unrequited love situation between Trey and Brian as well as their sexual experimentations on each other as adolescents, but doesn’t elaborate on it at all. She just leaves it there hanging. Possible homoerotic emotions between childhood friends who have ever since shared almost everything, including their women, sounds quite interesting to me and I would have liked to see how it turned out. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />And then there was Myrna’s ex, Jeremy. I was already too fed up with her and that awful conduct of hers (she had just hung up on Brian, being indescribably rude) when that call from Jeremy came. Her reactions after that were so preposterous I seriously considered not finishing this. <i>"Brian, I’m not calling you because I’m scared shitless, but because I don’t want you to come here"</i>, <i>"Brian, I don’t want you to stay on the phone with me … Oh well, just for a little bit"</i> and so on. Make up your mind, Myrna. You can’t be a bitch one minute and all wishy-washy, boo-hoo, please-protect-me the next.<br /><br />Then you have Brian, who takes the first plane to Kansas City to go save his damsel in distress and the first thing that crosses his mind when he sees another man holding her arm is that she’s cheating on him. I mean, enough already! <br /><br />That last 10% of the book was straight downhill until it hit rock bottom with the exchange of the necessary I-love-yous in such a nonchalant and childish way, it made Myrna’s whole no-L-word and no-strings-attached mentality up to that point seem utterly ridiculous. The woman is in serious need of therapy. I mean, years and years. Plus Brian could use the time in between to grow up.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15224586200613160003" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5430932724436741287"><b>4 to 41/2 stars</b><br/><br/>I'll admit I started this book only with the intention to curb my curiosity about what I've read in recent reviews and comments. I've noticed people either love this book or they don't. I was prepared to fall among those readers who do not like this story because I usually do not enjoy reading this type of erotica. I confess, my expectations were remarkably low. I neither expected nor was prepared for how fascinating, compelling, erotic, and, frankly, disturbing I found <i>Backstage </i></span>
  <span id="freeText5430932724436741287" style="display:none"><b>4 to 41/2 stars</b><br /><br />I'll admit I started this book only with the intention to curb my curiosity about what I've read in recent reviews and comments. I've noticed people either love this book or they don't. I was prepared to fall among those readers who do not like this story because I usually do not enjoy reading this type of erotica. I confess, my expectations were remarkably low. I neither expected nor was prepared for how fascinating, compelling, erotic, and, frankly, disturbing I found <i>Backstage Pass</i> to be. <br /><br />Although there was too much sex in this book (understatement of the century!) and at times the writing prose felt underdeveloped and stunted, the author did a great job giving the reader fun, endearing, and sexy characters; an intriguing plot; and a fairly realistic look at the lifestyle of a rock band. Their crass and seedy lifestyle fascinated, unsettled, and many times appalled me. Having said that, I still love so much about this book. <br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9767163091191588457">5 stars – Erotic Contemporary Romance<br/><br/>I love all kinds of music, including rock, but I’ve never been much of a concert groupie or band fan girl. Although my sister would probably call me a big fat liar and eagerly remind me of my closet New Kids On The Block phase as a teen. <i>*blushes and hides of embarrassment*</i><br/><br/>But I’ve definitely had my fair share of hot celeb obsessions, including Robert Pattinson (I stalked him on the Internet for months before and after <i>Twilight</i> came out!), Brad Pitt (I watche</span>
  <span id="freeText9767163091191588457" style="display:none">5 stars – Erotic Contemporary Romance<br /><br />I love all kinds of music, including rock, but I’ve never been much of a concert groupie or band fan girl. Although my sister would probably call me a big fat liar and eagerly remind me of my closet New Kids On The Block phase as a teen. <i>*blushes and hides of embarrassment*</i><br /><br />But I’ve definitely had my fair share of hot celeb obsessions, including Robert Pattinson (I stalked him on the Internet for months before and after <i>Twilight</i> came out!), Brad Pitt (I watched <i>Legends of the Fall</i> countless times), Antonio Sabato Jr. (Jagger Cates on <i>General Hospital</i> was a long time crush), Jason Statham (<i>Transporter</i>...hello!), and Vin Diesel (‘cause his rock hard body, bald head, and tatts totally do it for me) to name a few. So, I can certainly understand the inclination to obsess over sexy rock star gods like the Sinners.<br /><br /><b>Backstage Pass</b> totally kindled my Kindle and nearly set it on fire...it’s that freakin’ HOT! I mean seriously...YOWZA! It’s got a little bit of everything in the smutty fun, kink rainbow, including oral, anal, sex toys, light bondage, exhibitionism/voyeurism, ménage, mild m/m action (kissing and fondling), and oh yeah, vanilla vaginal sex, too. And when Brian felt music inspiration during sex and got all trancelike? <i>Whew</i>...it was extremely erotic. <br /><br />It’s definitely a 5+ star read in terms of its explosive hotness, but I didn’t really love the main characters. Brian was a sweet, sexy beta hero and a “Beast” in the bedroom, but his neediness got a little annoying at times. Myrna’s mix of stuffy, Ms. Uptight Professor on the outside and inner slut queen was funny, but her insecurity was irritating. I actually preferred the secondary characters, particularly goofy drummer Eric Sticks and sweet, sexy, bisexual guitarist Trey Mills. I’m sooo looking forward to Trey’s story, <b>Double Time</b>, but it’s the last book in the series and doesn’t come out until Oct’2012...wahhh. <br /><br />Even though I didn’t care all that much for the lead H/h, it’s still a solid 5 star read for the smutty good, scorching HOTness! And I’m really looking forward to the rest of the series! Lead singer Sedric Lionheart came across as a narcissistic, sex addicted egomaniac (you know, a rock star sex god?), so I’m anxious for his story that’s up next in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9442157.Rock_Hard__Sinners_on_Tour___2_" title="Rock Hard (Sinners on Tour, #2) by Olivia Cunning" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Hard</a>.<br /><br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_139743508" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/139743508" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2043222-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577660807p2/2043222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/139743508?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/2043222-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer139743508" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17729733179718690800">Review re-posted on <a href='http://wp.me/p3FyId-1he' rel='nofollow noopener'>Got Fiction?</a><br/><br/>I got this book for review, and it turns out it’s one I’ve read before! It looks like Sourcebooks is repackaging this series. If you like rockstar romance, I want to say this is the book that sort of kicked off that subgenre a few years ago.<br/><br/>I also want to say that once I realized I’d read this, I didn’t re-read it, so I”m not sure how it would hold up to my tastes now, 5 years later. Sometimes books really hold up well, sometimes they don’t. But here’s my original</span>
  <span id="freeText17729733179718690800" style="display:none">Review re-posted on <a href="http://wp.me/p3FyId-1he" rel="nofollow noopener">Got Fiction?</a><br /><br />I got this book for review, and it turns out it’s one I’ve read before! It looks like Sourcebooks is repackaging this series. If you like rockstar romance, I want to say this is the book that sort of kicked off that subgenre a few years ago.<br /><br />I also want to say that once I realized I’d read this, I didn’t re-read it, so I”m not sure how it would hold up to my tastes now, 5 years later. Sometimes books really hold up well, sometimes they don’t. But here’s my original review from 2011 that was posted on the old Demon Lover’s Books &amp; More site.<br /><br /><b>Original Review:</b><br /><br />I won this is a goodreads first reads contest! Woot!! Happy dance!<br /><br />I wasn't sure what to expect when I saw all the wonderful 4 and 5 star reviews for this book as it's not my normal fare. <br /><br />Let me tell you what to expect from this book:<br />*expect super hot, steamy, and naughty sex in the first few pages.<br />*expect a real plot, you heard me, A REAL PLOT<br />*expect a direct look into the lives of the Sinners<br />*expect more hot, steamy, naughty sex<br />*expect humor, that's right, this steamy bit of naughty goodness has some of the best scenes. My favorite (what does this say about me? lol) is where Brian and Myrna haven't seen each other in about a month, and they can't make it out of the airport without a steamy sex scene in a bathroom stall...interrupted by the guy in the next stall farting. OMGsh I laughed so hard I had tears rolling down my cheeks!<br /><br />Another awesome example is that due to the random bathroom guy, they couldn't finish so Myrna <i>gave Brian a hand</i> *wink wink* on the ride back to his tour bus, but used his lucky hat to cover what she was doing. His lucky hat became his <i>get</i> lucky hat and he gave it to his buddy....ummm...without wiping it out! You know that scene in There's Something About Mary, where she asks "Is that hair gel?" and uses it on her bangs? That is what I though of everytime I saw a scene with the lucky hat! <br /><br />So, now you've seen the big points in this book that I would never had though to see in an erotic romance. <br /><br />Moving on to the plot-quick review: Myrna is a human sexuality professor who loves the Sinners. Brian is the very drunk guitarist who she has a crush on. Myr wants a one night stand with her crush, Brian falls in love. How on earth will this work out? <br /><br />The only thing I didn't like was the threesome scene. I don't mean the way it was written because I think it was soo sexy, trust me, Olivia Cunning <i>can write</i>. It's just that it was so far into the book-it was towards end, by that point we know Brian and Myrna are in love and it ruined it for me. I expect that in the beginning and middle where it's still new and has less chance of ruining a relationship. But I also know it will not bother most readers, it really is just me. However I think we needed the revelation that happens during that scene-I'm hoping some of those loose ends will be used throughout the series. <br /><br />I wish more had been done with the abusive ex husband. I loved the end scene with the taser (evil grin here-but I won't spoil it for anyone else).<br /><br />The fact that Brian and Myrna hit it off so quickly was awesome, but I felt that the little things like Myrna cooking for the guys, and helping out Brian's relationship with his dad- So many touching scenes really made me feel that there was more than just smokin' hot sex between them. <br /><br />I can't wait for the next book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9442157.Rock_Hard__Sinners_on_Tour___2_" title="Rock Hard (Sinners on Tour, #2) by Olivia Cunning" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Hard</a> and I can't wait to see what happens now that Myrna knows <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trey is in love with Brian <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Olivia Cunning is an amazing new talent in the erotic romance field and I will read anything she writes. <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.com/2011/03/backstage-pass-by-olivia-cunning.html">http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.co...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17729733179718690800" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12496511994394126642">I shit you not!<br/>When I decided to start reading this story I had Avenged Sevenfold’s album “Nightmare” playing softly in the background…<br/> <br/><i> Really Kellie?? who are you shitting??.. It wasn’t playing softly, who plays Metal softly? It was LOUD.. but it was still in the background! Alright… </i> <br/><br/>So anyway!! <br/>While I was reading away in this book and falling for Brian, Sed, Trey, Jace and Eric I looked up some other reviews to see if anyone had any photos of how they envisioned Brian… As I couldn’t quite p</span>
  <span id="freeText12496511994394126642" style="display:none">I shit you not!<br>When I decided to start reading this story I had Avenged Sevenfold’s album “Nightmare” playing softly in the background…<br> <br><i> Really Kellie?? who are you shitting??.. It wasn’t playing softly, who plays Metal softly? It was LOUD.. but it was still in the background! Alright… </i> <br><br>So anyway!! <br>While I was reading away in this book and falling for Brian, Sed, Trey, Jace and Eric I looked up some other reviews to see if anyone had any photos of how they envisioned Brian… As I couldn’t quite picture him.. <br>as soon as I read that Sed wore Mirrored glasses and had DIMPLES! <br><i>(Goddamn Dimples get me every time!) </i><br>he was M.Shadows in my mind!<i>(YES I'm aware that M.Shadows was my Travis Maddox but come on I've got a crush ok?! LOL)</i><br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/seddimples_zps2e6483e4.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379752i/736163.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So I was super super psyched when I saw an interview with Olivia Cunning when she said that she had the idea for this series at an Avenged Sevenfold concert!! Be still my heart I think I love her!<br> <br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/a7x_zps4e080339.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379752i/736164.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> I got the original idea for Backstage Pass at an Avenged Sevenfold concert (no, not because I had a backstage pass… bummer…), so it’s only fitting that they were the original inspiration for Sinners. Once I got writing, I deviated from the real life band, especially personality-wise, as the fictional characters became more “real” to me than real-life rock stars, but yes, they were the original inspiration. Especially, Synyster Gates, M. Shadows and Zacky Vengeance. Yum-to-the-um.</i> Full interview can be found @ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://danicaavet.wordpress.com/2011/05/25/author-interview-olivia-cunning/">http://danicaavet.wordpress.com/2011/...</a><br><br>Then later it was mentioned Brian wears guyliner he become Jared to me <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/brianjaredleto_zpsb1a46ba7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379752i/736165.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anyway! <br><br><b>
  <u>THE STORY</u>
</b> <br><br>Myrna is sex psychiatrist, while being at a seminar she see’s the Sinners drinking in the bar. <br>She has long used Brian “Master” Sinclair’s riff’s while teaching. She knows this is the one chance she has to meet them she jumps at it. She doesn’t quite fit n with her stuffy suit and being 35 while they are all in their mid to late 20’s. <br><br>Turns out she was wrong, they all want a piece of her, but she only has eyes for Brian.<br><br>Brian is a hopeless romantic and is heartbroken and blind drunk after his latest girlfriend Angie, cheated on him with the lead singer Sed.<br><br> (They all seem to cheat on him with Sed)<br><br>She tells Brian her room number anyway and says she has what he needs. <br>He follows up and finds her room, but she just takes care of him, giving him Tylenol and vitamins for his hangover. <br><br>But in the morning…<br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/clickovariesexplode.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379752ra/736166.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brian finds that Myrna is his Muse! While they “make love” he hears the music, everytime! <br><br>One time he can’t find a pen so writes on her!<br><br><b>
  <i>“I'd cuddle with you, but I don't want to sweat off my riff and solo</i>
</b> <br><br>They spend <b>A LONG LONG LONG LONG TIME</b> “writing music” *wink wink* <br><br>Brian knows that she is the one for him…. Myrna has had a bad divorce and doesn’t want anything more than the weekend they have, before he goes back on tour. <br><br>At the end of the weekend Myrna, gets in her car and drives away.. <br><br>Leaving Brian at the tour bus without her number or even her surname… <br><br>Brian’s best friend Trey is sick of Brian moping around and tracks Myrna down for him.<br><br>Brian finally gets the courage to call and convinces her to come and see him, even paying for her flights. <br><br>When Myrna arrives she has a proposition for the band… <br><br>She has been given a grant for 10k to study groupies… <br> <br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/groupies_zps659ddb8a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379752i/736167._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She’ll continue to “have a good time” with Brian so he can write music, if they let her tour with them and interview their groupies for her study. <br><br>Of course the band agrees and the story goes from there…. <br><br>Sex, friendships, Cherry obsessions, shopping trips, bromances, flanter, home cooked meals, tour bus scandals, threesomes, stalkers, sec, groupies, suck circles, sex, beautiful music, sex, some more sex.<br>And a sweet HEA… <br><br><b>
  <u>MY THOUGHTS</u>
</b> <br><br><b> HOLY SCREAMING MUTIPLE ORGASMS BATMAN!!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/cool_down.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379752ra/736168.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What a wild fucking ride!!! <br><br>When you think of Rock bands what do you think of? <br><b><br>SEX, DRUGS, ROCK N ROLL, TATTOO’S, LEATHER, PIERCINGS?<br></b> <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/fuckyes.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379752ra/736169.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Well check all that off! <br>It’s DEF what we get!! Well not the drugs part.. A lot of Alcohol does that count? <br>I am totally 100% a Sinners Groupie! <br>It’s SMUT at it’s best! With Tattoo’d, pierced metal gods…<br>Yeah there was a bit of plot in between the sex scenes, Wasn't the strongest plot and didn’t really cover the Ex all that much but I still loved it. <br><br>Brian being a hopeless romantic broke my heart! I loved him! <br><br>I loved Myrna and how she made Brian feel! I loved how it was from several different POV’s. <br><br>I can’t wait to get into Sed, Trey <b>
  <i>ESPECIALLY THOSE TWO’S!</i>
</b> heads, Jace and Eric as well! <br><br>Who am I kidding I can’t wait to read the rest of the series.. <br><br>As a metal/emo/rock n roll loving chick this whole story was right up my alley.<br><br> The music talk, the feeling that I was actually at their concert! Also as a MASSIVE A7X fan I pretty much envisioned them while on stage! <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/a7xgif_zpsb1bea1fc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379752ra/736170.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The thing that annoyed me most was the damn errors! Soo many!I mean SHITLOADS!<br> <br>I am still going to give it 5 stars though… <br><br>Off to demolish Sed’s story now! <br><br><b>
  <u>QUOTE’S/CONVO’S/THOUGHTS I LIKED</u>
</b><br><b>
  <i><br><br>"We told you he was a romantic retard last night." <br>-Trey<br>*************<br>“He put his fingertips against her forehead.<br>"You must be at least this tall to ride The Beast."<br>"Secure your belongings and keep your arms and legs around the ride at all times.” <br>*************<br>“None of your business. Go get me a beer.” <br>“When did he pass out last night?" Eric asked Myrna.<br>"After he swallowed my banana and I forced him to consume my fluids.” <br>*************<br> “Deeper?         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer144368665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15511442516179911999">OK, I'm HOOKED. I am officially a Sinners groupie. Oh Brian and his magical fingers, he can pluck my strings anytime. Not only is he a musical genius, he is gorgeous, a one-woman man, and a hopeless romantic, what's not to love?! Of course, the book was dripping with sensuality, no pun intended, but it was a great story. Five young men achieving fame and fortune, and and having to deal with the overwhelming enormity of it all. No sense of normalcy, until Myrna comes into their lives. She falls f</span>
  <span id="freeText15511442516179911999" style="display:none">OK, I'm HOOKED. I am officially a Sinners groupie. Oh Brian and his magical fingers, he can pluck my strings anytime. Not only is he a musical genius, he is gorgeous, a one-woman man, and a hopeless romantic, what's not to love?! Of course, the book was dripping with sensuality, no pun intended, but it was a great story. Five young men achieving fame and fortune, and and having to deal with the overwhelming enormity of it all. No sense of normalcy, until Myrna comes into their lives. She falls for Brian and they all fall for her. Usually it's the men in the books that are older, but in this case Myrna is 7 years older than Brian, and I liked that. A lot of humorous moments, especially when they all decide to go grocery shopping. Too funny!<br /><br />I'm looking forward to the next book. I didn't like Sed in the beginning, but by the end of the book he was tugging at my heart. Dying to see what Olivia Cunning has in store for him. I'm holding my lighter up for the encore!!</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer135045873" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3141622599110658981">This book ROCKED!<br/><br/>First off I must say that if by chance that Olivia Cunning is reading this review, Thank You for writing such a fantastic story. I can hardly wait for the rest of this series to come out and will be reading Rock Hard as soon as it's released.<br/><br/>Second off Thank You Shawna, if you would not have been reading this book I would more than likely have missed out on this one.<br/><br/>This is by far the best Rock and Roll romance I've ever read. I absolutely adored everything about the hero Brian.</span>
  <span id="freeText3141622599110658981" style="display:none">This book ROCKED!<br /><br />First off I must say that if by chance that Olivia Cunning is reading this review, Thank You for writing such a fantastic story. I can hardly wait for the rest of this series to come out and will be reading Rock Hard as soon as it's released.<br /><br />Second off Thank You Shawna, if you would not have been reading this book I would more than likely have missed out on this one.<br /><br />This is by far the best Rock and Roll romance I've ever read. I absolutely adored everything about the hero Brian. This book was a book made of my wildest fantasy's. The love/sex scenes in this book alone deserve 5 stars and there was MANY of them. This is an erotic romance but what I find a lot in erotic romances with tons of sex in them is that as the book moves along the sex scenes all start sounding the same. That was not true with this book. The loves scenes were fresh and well thought out not to mention SCORCHING. I loved how the story explained all the characters in this book and their relationships with each other. That really wetted my appetite for MORE book's and I am happy knowing that the other members of this series are getting their stories too. The ending was so darn good that I had goose bumps all over my body and tears of happiness in my eye's.<br /><br />This book read like a Lorelei James book but with Rock Stars instead of Cowboy's. So I recommend this book to all those LJ fans out there. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/132642994?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cherrie Lynn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cherrie Lynn" href="/user/show/3160172-cherrie-lynn">Cherrie Lynn</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer132642994" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13578162564499955559">Oh, this book was so far up my alley, I don't even know where to begin. Olivia had me from the dedication, and she didn't let go. I loved Myrna from the moment I realized she recognizes the seething sexuality inherent in heavy metal music--something I think a lot of people don't get (and that's a shame, because it's an absolute goldmine). There might have been a couple of moments I wanted to smack her for her stubbornness, but that's only because I was madly in love with Brian and wanted to yell</span>
  <span id="freeText13578162564499955559" style="display:none">Oh, this book was so far up my alley, I don't even know where to begin. Olivia had me from the dedication, and she didn't let go. I loved Myrna from the moment I realized she recognizes the seething sexuality inherent in heavy metal music--something I think a lot of people don't get (and that's a shame, because it's an absolute goldmine). There might have been a couple of moments I wanted to smack her for her stubbornness, but that's only because I was madly in love with Brian and wanted to yell at her to hurry up and figure out that she was, too. :-) Ohh, Brian. He was smart, funny, sweet and indescribably hot. <br /><br />And who hasn't had this fantasy? It's something I think we can all relate to, but what made this book so awesome was that we see it unfold in a way that's real and, perhaps most importantly, believable. I was in heaven reading it. I'd also be remiss in not mentioning how hot it is. It isn't just hot, it's nuclear.<br /><br />But I have to say, as much as I love those sinfully sexy shredders, I go completely gaga for growling frontmen. So it should go without saying that I cannot WAIT for Sed's book! I'm looking forward to many, many more from Olivia.<br /><br />Rock on... \m/</span>

  <span id="freeText10982294680600012233" style="display:none">As smut goes, this was pretty fun porn. All about a metal band that tours the country to do shows and hump everything within a 10 mile radius. <br><br>And, I had to wonder: why would anyone want this as their life? It didn't seem glamorous, it seemed kind of depressing. Maybe it's the female in me or something, but I can't imagine anything worse than traveling in a filthy bus for months at a time. Ick! I can barely handle the smell after a 6 hour road trip with my family. What happens on a molecular level that brings about the funky smell of teenage and 20ish something boys?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459664066i/18640039._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>"Vacation" was really a documentary about what happens to parents stuck in the car with their kids for too long.</i><br><br>So, in this book, we have Myrna (nice name, grandma!), who is a college professor of Human Sexuality, and 35 yrs old. She has a one-night stand with Brian, the lead guitarist of the metal band, romantic boy, and 28 yrs old. He falls in love with her and they have a lot of sex. That's really the plot.<br><br>It was still some pretty good smut. There was a LOT of sex. Obviously. But, the best part was all of the band members who were each awesome in their own way. I'm going to continue reading more of this series. I need to do more investigating into the world of rock stars. For science.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459664066i/18640040.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Shut up, Zoidburg!</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10588701384231720705"><b>Holy Super Sexy Series Batman!!</b><br/>If you're looking for your next guilty pleasure, look no further!<br/>Rock Stars + Professor of Human Sexuality + a bit of romance + a whole lot of sex = Do not attempt to read this book in public.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382473949ra/5908853.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387325412ra/7578056.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let's get serious for a second...   <span id="freeText10588701384231720705" style="display:none"><b>Holy Super Sexy Series Batman!!</b><br>If you're looking for your next guilty pleasure, look no further!<br>Rock Stars + Professor of Human Sexuality + a bit of romance + a whole lot of sex = Do not attempt to read this book in public.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382473949ra/5908853.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387325412ra/7578056.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let's get serious for a second... There is very little that is <i>"serious"</i> about this book. It is <u>not</u> a literary masterpiece; it is a <i>seriously entertaining</i> piece of erotica, so lets not get our panties in a twist. Sit back and enjoy it.<br><br><b>I'd say that the unofficial breakdown is:<br>80% Super Steamy Sex<br> 8% Rock Star Antics<br> 7% Witty Dialogue<br> 5% Passable Plot Line</b><br><br>I was hooked from the moment Brian began "Hearing Music" during sex... And it was because he began writing the score <u>on</u> Mynra. How hot is that? Who doesn't reserve a tiny part of their brain for fantasizing about being someone's muse?<br><blockquote>“I'd cuddle with you, but I don't want to sweat off my riff and solo."<br>She laughed. "That must be the first time that excuse has ever been used to avoid after-sex cuddling.”</blockquote> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387648276i/7642256._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book could easily work as a stand alone work, but it is part of the Sinners on Tour series. I downloaded the second book in the series immediately - and I think that speaks more about my enjoyment of the book than any review could.<br><br>As a Side Note: <i>My husband enjoyed the book... Not that he read it, but he appreciated the effects of it.</i> ;)<br><br><b>
  <u>Some of my Favorite Moments:</u>
</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>“When did he pass out last night?” Eric asked Myrna.<br>“After he swallowed my banana and I forced him to consume my fluids.” She winked at him.<br>His mouth fell open. “What?”<br><br><b>“Hold this over your tits so Trey doesn’t knock his guitar out of tune with his hard on.”</b><br><br>“Myr, your mole is interrupting my solo”<br><br>“If I’m stupid enough to fall in love with you in twelve hours, I deserve to have my heart broken.”<br><br>“Did you just come in my hair?”<br>“I’m sorry,” Eric said. “You’re just so hot, Myrna. I had to come on you. I couldn’t help it.”<br><br>“You know what they say. Absence makes the heart grow fonder.”<br>“If my heart grows any fonder, it’s going to hop out of my chest and into yours.”<br>She melted. She scooted up his body to kiss him. “That’s the sweetest thing anyone’s ever said to me.”<br>“It sounds sort of fatal,” he murmured.”<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>

    <a title="willaful" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2833071-willaful"><img alt="willaful" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1382328800p2/2833071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/162492938?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="willaful" class="user" itemprop="url" name="willaful" href="/user/show/2833071-willaful">willaful</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=uxorious-hero">uxorious-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=older-woman-younger-man">older-woman-younger-man</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=sexy-beta">sexy-beta</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=o-performer-artist-creative">o-performer-artist-creative</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=fabulous-wallbanger">fabulous-wallbanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=mmf-fmm">mmf-fmm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=o-theatre-film-show-biz-celebrity">o-theatre-film-show-biz-celebrity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=o-teacher-professor">o-teacher-professor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=putting-the-fun-in-dysfunctional">putting-the-fun-in-dysfunctional</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer162492938" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15957031371007469695">You can tell I read a lot of romance and not much erotica, because when our heroine Myrna meets sexy rockstar Brian and all his sexily-named band-mates, my first innocent thought was, “Gee, I bet all those other guys are going to have their own stories later,” not “Woo hoo, I bet all those other guys are also going to get it on with Myrna!” As it turned out, the focus <i>is</i> on the primary relationship with Brian, though a couple of the other guys do come into the story, if you know what I mean and </span>
  <span id="freeText15957031371007469695" style="display:none">You can tell I read a lot of romance and not much erotica, because when our heroine Myrna meets sexy rockstar Brian and all his sexily-named band-mates, my first innocent thought was, “Gee, I bet all those other guys are going to have their own stories later,” not “Woo hoo, I bet all those other guys are also going to get it on with Myrna!” As it turned out, the focus <i>is</i> on the primary relationship with Brian, though a couple of the other guys do come into the story, if you know what I mean and I think you do.<br /><br />This was a kink smorgasbord, with a little bit of this and a little bit of that. Bondage, menage, anal, voyeurism, m/m, sex in public... I may have forgotten a few things. It was like the old saying about the weather -- if you don’t like the sex, just wait a few minutes. It was also a weirdly charming look at wild but lovable rockers on tour, if you could get past the nasty way they treat their groupies (including Brian.) There was a lot of fantasy going on, and if I have to ignore dubious hygiene, dubious safe sex and some “don’t try this at home” moments, I don’t see why that one aspect has to be so realistic.<br /><br />Also on the negative side, I didn’t buy Myrna being so hung up on her ex-husband’s nasty namecalling that she expects Brian to think she’s a whore for enjoying sex. She’s a professor of human sexuality for crying out loud; even if she was affected on an emotional level she should have known on an <i>intellectual</i> level that it was all nonsense.<br /><br />But overall, this was a very fun read, even for someone like me who prefers romances that don’t have sex scenes on 95% of the pages.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15957031371007469695" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1358269490185619110">WOW - I think this is the most "sex-full" book I've read. <br/><br/>BP is Olivia Cunning's first book covering the Rock Band "Sinners". The band consist of the following members: Brian Sinclair, lead guitarist; Sedric Lionheart, lead singer; Trey Mills, rhythm guitarist; Eric Sticks, drummer; and Jace Seymour, bass.<br/><br/><b>5 stars</b> for erotic - of the 378 pages, most are filled with hot-steamy sex scenes -- vanilla-bondage-ménage-anal-voyeurism-mild m/m- sex in public-oral-sex toys-and I'm sure I've left some out.</span>
  <span id="freeText1358269490185619110" style="display:none">WOW - I think this is the most "sex-full" book I've read. <br /><br />BP is Olivia Cunning's first book covering the Rock Band "Sinners". The band consist of the following members: Brian Sinclair, lead guitarist; Sedric Lionheart, lead singer; Trey Mills, rhythm guitarist; Eric Sticks, drummer; and Jace Seymour, bass.<br /><br /><b>5 stars</b> for erotic - of the 378 pages, most are filled with hot-steamy sex scenes -- vanilla-bondage-ménage-anal-voyeurism-mild m/m- sex in public-oral-sex toys-and I'm sure I've left some out. For me, this book was more erotic fiction than an actual romance story. The sex was more dominant than the romantic aspect. And for hot, simmering sex, this book is a 5!<br /><br /><b>2.5</b> for the romantic element of the story. The story’s main focus is on the relationship of lead guitarist Brian Sinclair and Dr. Myrna Evans, professor of Human Sexuality. The first time Myrna meets Brian it was instant animal attraction on her part, primal desire. And even though Brian is drunk, within the first 24 hours of their meeting, we have our first sizzling sex scene. These two were hot for each other and there followed the theme of this book. There was romance,<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and Brian declares his love for her after only one day! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but I felt it was more the animal attraction, primal desire. I just wasn’t feeling the romance with this one. <br /><br /><b>Coming Soon </b> - there will be an epilog to this book - <i>Appetite for Seduction</i> - and may be purchased from Olivia Cunning's website at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.oliviacunning.com">www.oliviacunning.com</a> for $.99 cents. It takes place 2 days after Backstage Pass and overlaps in time (but not content) with Rock Hard.<br /><br />This is a very popular book and there is even a website with bios, pictures and other information about this fictional band. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sinnersontour.com">www.sinnersontour.com</a><br /><br /><b>Brian Sinclair</b><br /> Lead Guitarist, Composer<br />Picture taken from Sinners webpage<br /> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Favorite Instrument: Schecter Hellraiser custom, black w/white flecks<br /> Born: February 21<br /> Vitals: Black hair, brown eyes, 5’10″ tall<br />Known for his finger-burning solos, some say Brian “Master” Sinclair was born with a guitar in his hands. While that isn’t exactly true, he did pick up the instrument at an early age. This is no surprise as his father is renowned guitarist, Malcolm O’Neal, of the 1970′s rock band, Winged Faith. Brian is a native of Southern California. He graduated from high school approximately ten years ago and started college to become a music teacher. When the band signed a contract with a major label in his freshman year, Brian quit school to tour with Sinners full-time.<br /> Previous bands: Lead guitarist for Crysys  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer135847570" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12693239298624502615"><br/><i>Backstage Pass</i> is the first book in Olivia Cunning’s <i>Sinners on Tour</i> series. It was also my <i>first</i> Olivia Cunning read, my <i>first</i> “rock star” read, my <i>first</i> ‘slightly older woman/younger man’ read, and my <i>first</i> super naughty read! I lost a lot of <i>first</i> virginities here, for sure! And I’ll let you in on a little secret - I didn’t even review this book back when I read it because I was embarrassed to admit I had read such a super naughty book… and <i>loved</i> it! I mean, **gasp** what would my husband say</span>
  <span id="freeText12693239298624502615" style="display:none"><br /><i>Backstage Pass</i> is the first book in Olivia Cunning’s <i>Sinners on Tour</i> series. It was also my <i>first</i> Olivia Cunning read, my <i>first</i> “rock star” read, my <i>first</i> ‘slightly older woman/younger man’ read, and my <i>first</i> super naughty read! I lost a lot of <i>first</i> virginities here, for sure! And I’ll let you in on a little secret - I didn’t even review this book back when I read it because I was embarrassed to admit I had read such a super naughty book… and <i>loved</i> it! I mean, **gasp** what would my husband say? His friends? My family? Well, those of you who know me know that I long ago stopped worrying about that! HA! Life’s too short to let others tell me what I can read and enjoy!!!<br /><br />Anyway, I won’t go into a bunch of details because there have been a bjillion awesome reviews already written. What I will say is that I loved the edginess of this story… the somewhat darker, forbiddenish world of a Rock and Roll band and their over-the-top sexual appetites. Yum!!<br /><br />I’d say if you’re looking for something different, give this a try, but the thing is, this is no longer different. There are many Rock Star books out there, but I’ll tell you this – I've yet to find one that even comes close to being as awesome as <i>Backstage Pass</i>! Why? Because there's a good, solid story here. No, I take it back! There's a <i>great</i> story here and the sex is just the icing on the already deliciously decadent cake! Brian Sinclair totally ROCKED my socks off!<br /></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=steam-sizzling">steam-sizzling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-contemporary">genre-contemporary</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer135053255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13492050488076050990">A scorching hot erotica with a pretty good story too. I'll admit I skimmed over some of the sex scenes as not everything in this book is my 'thing', but overall this was a great romantic/erotica read with two wonderful lead characters that made me laugh so many times. <br/><br/>Brian really fit the mold of a rocker. He was more of a lover than a fighter kind of guy, and his charm and devotion to Myrna was hot. Although sometimes he was bit too 'beta' for my tastes (did he really say 'pwease'?) he did fit </span>
  <span id="freeText13492050488076050990" style="display:none">A scorching hot erotica with a pretty good story too. I'll admit I skimmed over some of the sex scenes as not everything in this book is my 'thing', but overall this was a great romantic/erotica read with two wonderful lead characters that made me laugh so many times. <br /><br />Brian really fit the mold of a rocker. He was more of a lover than a fighter kind of guy, and his charm and devotion to Myrna was hot. Although sometimes he was bit too 'beta' for my tastes (did he really say 'pwease'?) he did fit perfectly in the context of this story. Myrna is a closet rocker chick who dresses in prim suits, she has a PhD in sexual psychology, and is even a few years older than Brian. When he meets her its instant attraction, and he quickly realizes she is quite possibly his muse. <br /><br />In my limited experience, it's a rare for an erotica book to have both a great story and sizzling hot sex scenes that don't feel cheesy or repetitive, but Olivia Cunning really pulled it off. <br /></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/155677384?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=menage">menage</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer155677384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10985013288846296930"><i>Adult review for erotic content</i><br/><br/>3.5 stars. Second Read 06/12 with the SM girls<br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Nnggnn," she groaned.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Nnggnn, indeed.<br/><br/>I keep wavering between a 3 and a 4 star rating. For erotica, it's pretty consistent with the amount of sexual scenarios, which I know did shock some people who thought this book was contemporary romance. Don't be fooled. There's going to be acts of voyeurism, light BDSM, threesomes, anal play, etc. packed into this book. It is a story about rock stars and their lifestyle</span>
  <span id="freeText10985013288846296930" style="display:none"><i>Adult review for erotic content</i><br /><br />3.5 stars. Second Read 06/12 with the SM girls<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Nnggnn," she groaned.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Nnggnn, indeed.<br /><br />I keep wavering between a 3 and a 4 star rating. For erotica, it's pretty consistent with the amount of sexual scenarios, which I know did shock some people who thought this book was contemporary romance. Don't be fooled. There's going to be acts of voyeurism, light BDSM, threesomes, anal play, etc. packed into this book. It is a story about rock stars and their lifestyle. If you've ever watched an episode of <i>Behind the Music</i> you'll get the idea.<br /><br />As an erotica, I'd give it a solid 4 star. As a read for the sake of entertainment, I'd stick closer to 3 or 3.25ish. The plot does take a while to develop but I loved going back on tour with the sinners and remembering where and why I fell in love with Brian (and Trey) in the first place.<br /><br />Myrna never really did it for me. I was surprised to find that she didn't annoy me on the second read but I didn't find myself gaining any sort of appreciation for her either. She was just a vehicle used by me in order to gain access to Brian. Maybe I'm a true Sinners groupie, then. <br /><br />There were a few moments that forced me to have to remember to suspend belief because it is erotica, after all. Although, I can buy into multiple orgasms faster than I can buy into kissing with morning breath! Don't read this unless you've read the book : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the scene where they kissed not long after he'd been rimming her...how did I miss that the first time around?!? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I remember thinking the first time I read the book that it was bizarre how Brian would write music during sex. During the second read I really enjoyed these scenes.<br /><br />In my original review, I pointed out how I could never date a rock star and this hasn't changed. It's crazy how psycho the groupies get. It would be way too hard to be with someone who is adored and stalked by so many people.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Of course not. But this is Sed Lionheart we're talking about here. You know? If he stepped in dog shit, I'd lick it off his boot if he asked me to.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />I don't doubt there are groupies like this out there. I'll have to say that chasing the dream of being with a rock star is much more safe in a book.<br /><br /><b>Original Review March 2011</b><br /><br />It was a fun book - I got to go on tour with a rock band by proxy without all of the drama of having to do it for real. There is no way I could date a rock star, no matter how much he 'loved' me. Nope. Couldn't do it. I am just not that trusting to think I could leave any person alone with molesting fans and not have the man's defenses worn down at one point.<br /><br />What did that have to do with the book? Absolutely nothing...that was just me thinking to myself.<br /><br />Steamy this book was (Yoda much?). I was glad to see a story develop after a start pretty much focused on only sex (yep...erotica. check.). Surprisingly, I wanted to know more about the backstory of some of the other band members, which means yep - guess I'll be reading more to the series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10985013288846296930" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7l0WJIaCTtSXy7Y5mCbARbEuNSy33ZHj0ygANJYsNBLUe3/2PdyHvDDgAlhv08qaZ3HS5HlQH4SIVkaFW2/GiA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aOTeS8taJUb804vVhvn9Lu8RkQUUbzDudJUWhUYXFENSwreZcATsLlv4P7RxDPfxOU52zdrivokv61A0i1Tm2Q==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer17166840174209458407">Combining her love for romantic fiction and rock ‘n roll, Olivia Cunning writes erotic romance centered around rock musicians. Raised on hard rock music from the cradle, she attended her first Styx concert at age six and fell instantly in love with live music. She's been known to travel over a thousand miles just to see a favorite band in concert. As a teen, she discovered her second love, romanti</span>
  <span id="freeText17166840174209458407" style="display:none">Combining her love for romantic fiction and rock ‘n roll, Olivia Cunning writes erotic romance centered around rock musicians. Raised on hard rock music from the cradle, she attended her first Styx concert at age six and fell instantly in love with live music. She's been known to travel over a thousand miles just to see a favorite band in concert. As a teen, she discovered her second love, romantic fiction -- first, voraciously reading steamy romance novels and then penning her own. Growing up as the daughter of a career soldier, she's lived all over the country and overseas. She recently moved to Galveston, Texas.</span>
